function debugSystemConstants() {
  console.log("=== DEBUG SYSTEM CONSTANTS ===");
  console.log("window.systemConstants:", window.systemConstants);
  console.log("window.systemConstants.constants:", window.systemConstants?.constants);
  console.log("VARIAVEL_PD:", window.systemConstants?.constants?.VARIAVEL_PD);
  console.log("VARIAVEL_PS:", window.systemConstants?.constants?.VARIAVEL_PS);
  console.log("=== FIM DEBUG ===");
}
